     <div id="omnicontent"> 
      <h3>UCR Reaccreditation by Western Association of Schools and Colleges (WASC)</h3> 
      <p>The UCR campus has been accredited since 1956; reaccreditation of the campus by the Western Association of Schools and Colleges (WASC) occurs approximately every ten years. UCR was most recently reaccredited on March 3, 2010; <a href="/docs/Reaccrediationletter03-10.pdf">see letter from WASC to Chancellor White</a>. UCR's next proposal for reaccreditation is due to be submitted to WASC in fall 2016. This website contains details of the last cycle of the reaccreditation process.</p> 
      <p>Steven Brint, Vice Provost for Undergraduate Education, is UCR's Accreditation Liaison Officer, the official representative of the campus to WASC.He can be reached by telephone at 951-827-7750. Key information can be found in the menu on the left.</p> 
     </div>

      <h2><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/79178681035/spotlight-campus-apartment-resident-association">Spotlight: Campus Apartment Resident Association</a></h2> 
      <div class="metadata"> 
       <span class="metalink date">March 10, 2014</span> 
       <span class="metalink note"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/79178681035/spotlight-campus-apartment-resident-association#notes" title="Notes">3 notes</a></span> 
       <a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/79178681035/spotlight-campus-apartment-resident-association" class="metalink permalink"> Full Story</a> 
       <span class="metalink tags"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/cara" class="taglink"> cara</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/campus-apartment-resident-association" class="taglink"> campus apartment resident association</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/get-involved" class="taglink"> get involved</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/rubi" class="taglink"> rubi</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/spotlight" class="taglink"> spotlight</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/ucr" class="taglink"> ucr</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/uc-riverside" class="taglink"> uc riverside</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/campus-apartments" class="taglink"> campus apartments</a></span> 
       <div class="clear"></div> 
      </div> 
      <p><span><img src="https://31.media.tumblr.com/51b6f192e02bb1aae7d456241c109e86/tumblr_inline_n28eqeer8H1r08h92.jpg" /></span></p> 
      <p><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/UCR-Campus-Apartment-Resident-Association/210886378984840" target="_blank"><em>Source.</em></a></p> 
      <p id="docs-internal-guid-627115c8-ad12-73cd-2a17-e0f9750ba903"><span>I started my time at UC Riverside four years ago, knowing absolutely no one and nothing about the area. Before I even moved into my freshman dorm room I decided I needed to join an organization on campus, seeing as it was how I made some of my good friends in high school. With so many options it was difficult to choose, but I decided to literally stay close to home and become part of the <a href="http://rhaucr.wordpress.com/" target="_blank">Residence Hall Association </a>for Aberdeen-Inverness. </span></p> 
      <p><span>The Residence Hall Association was sort of like the student government of the dorm residences. They filled orders for repairs, planned events and generally made living in the dorm halls more enjoyable. RHA is limited to those who live in campus dorms, though, so after my freshmen year I had no choice but to leave the organization. My second year passed by in a blur and it wasn’t until my third year that I heard about the <a href="http://housing.ucr.edu/residential-life/resident-associations.aspx" target="_blank">Campus Apartment Resident Association</a>, the sister org to RHA. Doing what RHA does but to a for a larger amount of people, CARA offered me another opportunity to improve the community I was living in, plan events and meet people with the same interests as mine. </span></p> 
      <p class="read_more_container"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/79178681035/spotlight-campus-apartment-resident-association" class="read_more">Read More</a></p> 
      <div class="clear"></div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- End Text Posts -->

     <!-- Text Posts --> 
     <div class="textpost entry"> 
      <div class="metadata"> 
       <span class="metalink date">March 10, 2014</span> 
       <a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/79173548759/so-you-said-its-only-for-medical-necessity-so-then" class="metalink permalink"> Full Story</a> 
       <span class="metalink tags"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/answers" class="taglink"> answers</a></span> 
       <div class="clear"></div> 
      </div> 
      <p><b>Anonymous asked: So you said it's only for medical necessity so then that means it's less likely for someone who doesn't have a medical necessity to get their single room. I'm just scared of getting a roommate because I'm not good at talking &amp; I fear sleeping with strangers in a room</b></p> 
      <p>I totally understand your concern because living with someone new, on top of moving to an unfamiliar place, is all sorts of weird and unfamiliar and just a little terrifying. What you’re feeling is totally normal, and a lot of other people you’ll meet in the residence halls feel the exact same way. It’s okay to feel scared — I really feel like 90% of my college experience has involved feeling afraid of one thing or another, and the other 10% is free food — but I really encourage you to look at this as an opportunity to get to know your very first person in a college setting. If your roommate releases his or her information before move-in day, you’ll have an opportunity to speak ahead of time via Facebook or email.</p> 
      <p>Some easy topics to get the conversation started and establish your relationship as people sharing a living space: Where are you from? Do you like it there? Have you shared a room before? Are you going to be okay if I have to wake up early? Do you mind if I keep a light on and study late? Can you give me a heads-up if you bring friends over? Do you mind if I bring friends over? (Ask this one before you actually bring them over, not when they’re right outside the door.) If you ever want to borrow something, can you please ask and let me know? Here’s my phone number in case you need to reach me — can I please have yours, too? I know it sounds kind of silly to point out, but these things are not okay: (x, y, z. Wearing my clothes without asking, eating my food without asking, going through my things, not respecting my space). I want to respect your space, too — is there anything you want me to know?</p> 
      <p>I know I’ve mentioned this before, but your RA (Resident Assistant) is going to be an invaluable resource to help you work through your concerns and talk to someone in a safe and welcoming environment. Your RA is literally there to help you feel better transitioning into dorm life, and if you ever feel like you don’t know how to talk to your roommate or feel uncomfortable about living with a stranger, your RA can help you get to know your roommate — and the other people in your hall — so maybe you won’t feel like you’re in a hall with strangers, but are instead supported by friends.</p> 
      <p>If you don’t feel like you can do this, I do recommend contacting Housing and speaking with someone about the requirements for a single room. Share your concerns and indicate your interest and reasoning for being placed in a single. You can always email them at housinginfo@ucr.edu.</p> 
      <p>But honestly, if you do end up sharing a space with someone, just consider their needs and how those needs relate to yours. Of course you might need to study late — so just keep your desk light on, and let your roommate know you need to work on things. Of course you might have to wake up early to catch a class while your roommate gets to sleep in late — let him or her know so they can expect to hear your alarm. You might not even totally click with your roommate. That’s okay. Not everyone becomes uber-best-friends. That’s okay. You’re a team in this room, not enemies, and not necessarily strangers. You’re working toward the common goal of sharing your room and making it feel like a miniature home. If you communicate your needs, and bring your concerns to your RA as they come up, you’ll have all the resources you need to make this a truly stellar year.</p> 
      <p>Good luck!</p> 
      <p>More answers below.</p> 
      <p class="read_more_container"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/79173548759/so-you-said-its-only-for-medical-necessity-so-then" class="read_more">Read More</a></p> 
      <div class="clear"></div>

       <span class="metalink date">March 06, 2014</span> 
       <span class="metalink note"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78792598220/hi-how-can-we-apply-for-a-position-here-at-life-at#notes" title="Notes">2 notes</a></span> 
       <a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78792598220/hi-how-can-we-apply-for-a-position-here-at-life-at" class="metalink permalink"> Full Story</a> 
       <span class="metalink tags"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/answers" class="taglink"> answers</a></span> 
       <div class="clear"></div> 
      </div> 
      <p><b>Anonymous asked: Hi! How can we apply for a position here at Life at UCR? Do you guys have any open positions right now? If so, what are the requirements to apply?</b></p> 
      <p>If you’re interested in contributing to the blog, we’re always considering applications. Please email a resume and writing sample to ucrstudentblog@gmail.com. Bonus: Staff writers are eligible for internship credit.</p> 
      <p>Requirements include the ability to write clearly and with skill, a general fondness for UCR and the ability to meet deadlines and reply to emails. Please include in your application if you’re involved in anything on campus, and sass/humor is an added bonus.</p>

      <h2><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78727042754/point-of-view-for-the-fitness-buffs">Point of View: For the Fitness Buffs</a></h2> 
      <div class="metadata"> 
       <span class="metalink date">March 05, 2014</span> 
       <span class="metalink note"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78727042754/point-of-view-for-the-fitness-buffs#notes" title="Notes">7 notes</a></span> 
       <a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78727042754/point-of-view-for-the-fitness-buffs" class="metalink permalink"> Full Story</a> 
       <span class="metalink tags"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/point-of-view" class="taglink"> point of view</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/ucr" class="taglink"> ucr</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/uc-riverside" class="taglink"> uc riverside</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/fitness-buffs" class="taglink"> fitness buffs</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/ucr-fitness" class="taglink"> ucr fitness</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/src" class="taglink"> src</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/ucr-src" class="taglink"> ucr src</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/delaynie" class="taglink"> delaynie</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/spotlight" class="taglink"> spotlight</a></span>

      <h2><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78595037986/why-i-chose-ucr">Why I Chose UCR</a></h2> 
      <div class="metadata"> 
       <span class="metalink date">March 04, 2014</span> 
       <span class="metalink note"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78595037986/why-i-chose-ucr#notes" title="Notes">16 notes</a></span> 
       <a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78595037986/why-i-chose-ucr" class="metalink permalink"> Full Story</a> 
       <span class="metalink tags"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/jessica" class="taglink"> jessica</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/why-i-chose-ucr" class="taglink"> why i chose ucr</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/why-ucr" class="taglink"> why ucr</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/ucr" class="taglink"> ucr</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/uc-riverside" class="taglink"> uc riverside</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/spotlight" class="taglink"> spotlight</a></span> 
       <div class="clear"></div> 
      </div> 
      <p><img alt="image" src="https://31.media.tumblr.com/de4beb3462ab8eadeedde808895171c3/tumblr_inline_n1xsrgLhNS1r08h92.png" /></p> 
      <p><a href="http://instagram.com/lifeatucr" target="_blank"><em>Source.</em></a></p> 
      <p><span>“Why did you choose UC Riverside?” isn’t a question I get asked often enough, and when I am asked, I don’t say nearly enough. I was a high school senior in northern California three years ago, and at my high school, it’s a huge trend to move far away from home. A lot of my friends were getting into schools like Cal Poly SLO, UC Irvine, UC Berkeley, UCLA, UCSD, MIT, Johns Hopkins … I think you get the picture.</span></p> 
      <p>But before we get to the part where I actually decided where to go to college, let’s talk about my college selection process. I didn’t apply out of state. I didn’t want to put my parents under the financial burden of paying out-of-state tuition, especially since I was a pretty average student and not exactly the most active. All of the schools I applied to were in California, and the majority of them were UCs. I knew my chances weren’t bleak, but I also knew they weren’t amazing.</p> 
      <p class="read_more_container"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78595037986/why-i-chose-ucr" class="read_more">Read More</a></p> 
      <div class="clear"></div> 
     </div>

       <blockquote>

      <h2><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78482317693/a-day-in-the-life-rebecca">A Day in the Life: Rebecca</a></h2> 
      <div class="metadata"> 
       <span class="metalink date">March 03, 2014</span> 
       <span class="metalink note"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78482317693/a-day-in-the-life-rebecca#notes" title="Notes">9 notes</a></span> 
       <a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78482317693/a-day-in-the-life-rebecca" class="metalink permalink"> Full Story</a> 
       <span class="metalink tags"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/a-day-in-the-life" class="taglink"> a day in the life</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/day-in-the-life" class="taglink"> day in the life</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/rebecca" class="taglink"> rebecca</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/spotlight" class="taglink"> spotlight</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/ucr" class="taglink"> ucr</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/uc-riverside" class="taglink"> uc riverside</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/college" class="taglink"> college</a><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/highlander-newspaper" class="taglink"> highlander newspaper</a></span> 
       <div class="clear"></div> 
      </div> 
      <p><img alt="image" src="https://31.media.tumblr.com/f19884b7531156a68a7266d8ed25a856/tumblr_inline_n1oezfAt351r08h92.jpg" /></p> 
      <p>Alright, ladies and gentlemen. My day-to-day schedule is weird and packed and altogether funky, but I’m making all the other writers put this together, so here’s mine: a <a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/tagged/a-day-in-the-life" target="_blank">day in my life</a>. A Tuesday, to be exact.</p> 
      <p class="read_more_container"><a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/post/78482317693/a-day-in-the-life-rebecca" class="read_more">Read More</a></p>

    (function(){
        var analytics_frame = document.getElementById('ga_target');
        var analytics_iframe_loaded;
        var user_logged_in;
        var blog_is_nsfw = 'No';

        var eventMethod = window.addEventListener ? "addEventListener" : "attachEvent";
        var eventer = window[eventMethod];
        var messageEvent = eventMethod == "attachEvent" ? "onmessage" : "message";
        eventer(messageEvent,function(e) {
            var message = (e.data && e.data.split) ? e.data.split(';') : '';
            switch (message[0]) {
                case 'analytics_iframe_loaded':
                    analytics_iframe_loaded = true;
                    postCSMessage();
                    postGAMessage();
                    break;
                case 'user_logged_in':
                    user_logged_in = message[1];
                    postGAMessage();
                    break;
            }
        }, false);

        analytics_frame.src = "http://assets.tumblr.com/analytics.html?dc636e9b34dfd27b194aed14513506cb#http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com"
        function postGAMessage() {
            if (analytics_iframe_loaded && user_logged_in) {
                var is_ajax = false;
                analytics_frame.contentWindow.postMessage(['tick_google_analytics', is_ajax, user_logged_in, blog_is_nsfw, '/?route=%2F'].join(';'), analytics_frame.src.split('/analytics.html')[0]);
            }
        }
        function postCSMessage() {
            COMSCORE = true;
            analytics_frame.contentWindow.postMessage('enable_comscore;' + window.location, analytics_frame.src.split('/analytics.html')[0]);
        }
    })();
</script>

            YUI().use("node", function(Y){
              var masterElement = Y.one("#mediaattwidgetroncached");
              var frag = Y.one(document.createDocumentFragment());
              var alts = masterElement.all("> .alt-tabs > .tab");
              var tabsElement = masterElement.one(".tabs");
              var wraps = masterElement.all(".wrap");
              var i = 0;
              wraps.each(function(wrap) {
                var widget = wrap.one(" > *:first-child");
                if (widget) {
                  (!widget.hasClass("widget")) && widget.addClass("widget");
                  var tab = widget.one("> .tab");
                  tab = (tab != null) ? tab : ((alts && alts.size() > i) ? alts.item(i) : null);
                  if (tab != null) {
                    tab.setStyle("display","block");
                    var nnode = frag.create("<div class='tab-wrap'></div>");
                    nnode.append(tab.cloneNode(true));
                    widget.setAttribute("data-tab-id", nnode.generateID());
                    frag.append(nnode);
                    tab.remove();
                  }
                }
                i++;
              });
              if (tabsElement !== null) {
                tabsElement.append(frag);
              }
              masterElement.setAttribute("data-preloaded", "1");
            });

        // Google WaterMark Script
        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {
                ToggleHint($(this)); // add class on page load to elements with "hintable" class
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }
    </script>

     <div class="span-18 last"> 
      <h3>How To Order Transcripts</h3> 
      <p>You can order transcripts online, by mail or in person. </p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-18 last"> 
      <div class="padding"> 
       <div class="tabs"> 
        <table class="tabs gray"> 
         <tbody>
          <tr> 
           <td id="tab1" class="selected">ONLINE</td> 
           <td id="tab2">BY MAIL</td> 
           <td id="tab3">IN PERSON</td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody>
        </table> 
        <table class="nav"> 
         <tbody>
          <tr> 
           <td colspan="3"></td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody>
        </table> 
       </div> 
       <div class="tab-content"> 
        <div id="tab1-content"> 
         <p>Current students and alumni may order and pay for transcripts online via <a href="https://ucribm.ucr.edu/Paws/PAWS.html" target="_blank">Growl</a>. You will need your student identification number (SID) and permanent personal identification number (PERMPIN).</p> 
         <ul class="orange-bullets wide"> 
          <li><strong>Forget your PERMPIN?</strong> Call us at 951-827-7284 or come to the Highlander One Stop Shop (HOSS) on the first floor of the <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html?loc=SSB" target="_blank">Student Services Building</a>. A valid photo ID is required.</li> 
          <li><strong>Forget your SID?</strong> Log in to <a href="https://ucribm.ucr.edu/Paws/PAWS.html" target="_blank">Growl</a> with your SSN and PERMPIN and you will be able to retrieve your SID. </li> 
         </ul> 
        </div> 
        <div id="tab2-content" class="hide"> 
         <p> We only release transcripts upon receipt of a student-signed request. Print a <a href="/content/pdfs/transcript_request_form.pdf" target="_blank">Transcript Request Form</a> or create a letter (not an email) that includes the following: </p> 
         <ul class="orange-bullets wide"> 
          <li>Name(s) under which you attended</li> 
          <li>Student ID number</li> 
          <li>Date of birth</li> 
          <li>Dates of attendance (approximate if necessary)</li> 
          <li>Current address</li> 
          <li>Address(es) where transcripts are to be sent</li> 
          <li>Signature</li> 
         </ul> 
         <p><strong>Payment is due in advance for all transcript services.</strong> Include a check or money order payable to &quot;UC Regents&quot; with your Transcript Request Form. See the fees section for a breakdown of the costs.</p> 
         <p><strong>Please mail </strong>your Transcript Request Form and check or money order to:</p> 
         <address> University of California, Riverside<br /> Office of the Registrar<br /> 900 University Ave.<br /> Riverside, CA 92521<br /> </address> 
        </div> 
        <div id="tab3-content" class="hide"> 
         <p><strong>Print a <a href="/content/pdfs/transcript_request_form.pdf" target="_blank">Transcript Request Form</a> </strong>or pick one up at <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html?loc=SSB" target="_blank">the HOSS</a>.</p> 
         <p><strong>Take your completed Transcript Request Form </strong>to the Cashier's Office (at the HOSS) and pay with cash, check or money order made payable to &quot;UC Regents.&quot; </p> 
         <p> <strong>A valid photo ID</strong> is required.</p> 
         <p><strong>The Cashier's Office is open</strong> from 9 a.m.-12 p.m. and 1-3 p.m. The drop box is available until 4 p.m.</p> 
         <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <p>&nbsp;</p> 
       <h3>Fees</h3> 
       <table class="fees"> 
        <thead> 
         <tr> 
          <td><strong>Fee</strong></td> 
          <td><strong>Cost</strong></td> 
         </tr> 
        </thead> 
        <tbody> 
         <tr> 
          <td>Official Transcript </td> 
          <td>$10 per transcript</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>Rush Order</td> 
          <td>Additional $10 per order</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>Express Mail (Domestic)</td> 
          <td>Additional $19.95 per address</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>Express Mail (International)</td> 
          <td>Additional $44.95 per address</td> 
         </tr> 
         <tr> 
          <td>Fax Service</td> 
          <td>Additional $2 per page (Please call for total number of pages)</td> 
         </tr> 
        </tbody> 
       </table> 
      </div> 
      <h3>Processing Time</h3> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets wide"> 
       <li>Requests should be made <strong>two weeks before</strong> the transcript is needed.</li> 
       <li>Requests are processed within five to seven business days. Rush orders are processed within one business day.</li> 
       <li>Processing time <strong>DOES NOT</strong> include mail time.</li> 
       <li>A valid picture ID is required at the time of pick up.</li> 
      </ul> 
      <h3>Please Remember:</h3> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets wide"> 
       <li>You may not request a transcript by phone, email or fax. </li> 
       <li>You may not request a faxed transcript online.</li> 
       <li>You may not request internationally-mailed transcripts online.</li> 
       <li>UCR does not provide electronic transcript services or unofficial transcripts. You may, however, log in to <a href="https://ucribm.ucr.edu/Paws/PAWS.html" target="_blank">Growl</a> and print term grade reports. </li>
       <li>If transcripts are not picked up within 30 business days, another order must be placed.</li> 
       <li>All UCR debts (except long-term loans) must be paid before transcripts are released.</li> 
      </ul> 
      <h3>Questions?</h3> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets wide"> 
       <li>If you have questions, please <a href="mailto:lora.moore@ucr.edu?subject=Transcript%20Desk">email the Transcript Desk</a> or call (951) 827-7284. </li> 
       <li>For recorded information about transcripts, call the transcript information line at (951) 827-3400.</li> 
      </ul> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </div>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
